#                            Version compatibility: 0.1.0b1

#
#   These are the unit test records which should all correctly following any changes
#   in the program. Really. All of them. If the program is working correctly, the
#   output will terminate at FINAL-RECORD: "ALL OF THE UNIT TESTS WERE CODED CORRECTLY.
#   then "Exiting: <Stop> record "
#
#   These are a combination of tests of specific features, mostly with stylized sentences,
#   and assorted cases that broke earlier versions of the program for idiosyncratic reasons.  
#   The sentence IDs in this file may or may not correspond to those in other validation
#   files. Sorry.
#

<!-- Simple coding: this is the `first light'/"Hello World!" record -->
<!-- minus the final subordinate clause -->
<EventCoding sourcecode="ARN" targetcode="GON" eventcode="064">
<Text>
Arnor is about to restore full diplomatic ties with Gondor almost 
five years after crowds trashed its embassy.
</Text>
<Parse>
(ROOT
  (S
    (S
      (NP (NNP Arnor))
      (VP (VBZ is)
        (VP (IN about)
          (S
            (VP (TO to)
              (VP (VB restore)
                (NP (JJ full) (JJ diplomatic) (NNS ties))
                (PP (IN with)
                  (NP (NNP Gondor)))
                (SBAR
                  (NP (RB almost) (CD five) (NNS years))
                  (IN after)
                  (S
                    (NP (NNS crowds))
                    (VP (VBD trashed)
                      (NP (PRP$ its) (NN embassy)))))))))))
    (. .)))
</Parse>
</Sentence>

              (NP (NNP Wednesday)))))

          (NP
            (NP (NNS meetings))

<Sentence date="19950106" id="DEMO-06" category="DEMO">

<EventCoding sourcecode="CALGOV" targetcode="ITH" eventcode="050">
<Text>
The Calenardhon government condemned an attack by Osgiliath soldiers

</Text>

(ROOT
  (S
    (NP (DT The) (JJ Calenardhon) (NN government))
    (VP
      (VP (VBD condemned)
        (NP (DT an) (NN attack))
        (PP (IN by)
          (NP
            (NP (NNP Osgiliath) (NNS soldiers))
            (PP (IN in)
              (NP (JJ south) (NNP Ithilen)))))
        (PP (IN on)
          (NP (NNP Thursday))))
      (CC and)
      (VP (VBD promised)
        (NP (NN aid))
        (PP (TO to)
          (NP (DT the) (VBN affected) (NN Ithilen) (NNS villages)))))
    (. .)))
</Parse>
</Sentence>

<Sentence date="19950107" id="DEMO-07" category="DEMO">
<!-- [Compound target] -->
<EventCoding sourcecode="ARN" targetcode="DAG" eventcode="023">
<EventCoding sourcecode="ARN" targetcode="OSG" eventcode="023">
<Text>
Arnor believes Dagolath and Osgiliath can cope with a decrease in vital 
water from the mighty Entwash river when a major dam is filled next 
month. 
</Text>
<Parse>
(ROOT
  (S
    (NP (NNP Arnor))
    (VP (VBZ believes)
      (SBAR
        (S
          (NP (NNP Dagolath)
            (CC and)
            (NNP Osgiliath))
          (VP (MD can)
            (VP (VB cope)
              (PP (IN with)
                (NP
                  (NP (DT a) (NN decrease))
                  (PP (IN in)
                    (NP (JJ vital) (NN water)))))
              (PP (IN from)
                (NP
                  (NP (DT the) (JJ mighty) (JJ Entwash) (NN river))
                  (SBAR
                    (WHADVP (WRB when))
                    (S
                      (NP (DT a) (JJ major) (NN dam))
                      (VP (VBZ is)
                        (VP (VBN filled)
                          (NP-TMP (JJ next) (NN month)))))))))))))
    (. .)))
</Parse>
</Sentence>

<Sentence date="19950108" id="DEMO-08" category="DEMO">
<!-- [Compound actor list; however, note that the agent AMBASSADORS is -->
<!-- not carried through to the other actors. Also see COMPOUND-24] -->
<EventCoding sourcecode="ARNGOV" targetcode="ITHGOVPRS" eventcode="032">
<EventCoding sourcecode="OSG" targetcode="ITHGOVPRS" eventcode="032">
<EventCoding sourcecode="GON" targetcode="ITHGOVPRS" eventcode="032">
<Text>
The ambassadors of Arnor, Osgiliath and Gondor presented 
credentials to Ithilen's president on Wednesday in a further 
show of support to his government by their countries. 
</Text>
<Parse>
(ROOT
  (S
    (NP
      (NP (DT The) (NNS ambassadors))
      (PP (IN of)
        (NP (NNP Arnor) (, ,) (NNP Osgiliath)
          (CC and)
          (NNP Gondor))))
    (VP (VBD presented)
      (NP (NNS credentials))
      (PP (TO to)
        (NP
          (NP
            (NP (NNP Ithilen) (POS 's))
            (NN president))
          (PP (IN on)
            (NP
              (NP (NNP Wednesday))
              (PP (IN in)
                (NP
                  (NP (DT a) (JJ further) (NN show))
                  (PP (IN of)
                    (NP (NN support)))))))))
      (PP (TO to)
        (NP (PRP$ his) (NN government)))
      (PP (IN by)
        (NP (PRP$ their) (NNS countries))))
    (. .)))
    
<!--Coreference set:
	(12,27,[27,28)) -> (12,2,[1,9)), that is: "their" -> "The ambassadors of Arnor , Osgiliath and Gondor"
-->
</Parse>
</Sentence>

<Sentence date="19950101" id="AGENT-01" category="AGENT" valid="true">
<!-- One-word suffixed agent following [source] actor  -->
<EventCoding sourcecode="ARNMOS" targetcode="GON" eventcode="064">
<Text>
Arnor cleric is about to restore full diplomatic ties with Gondor almost 
five years after crowds trashed its embassy.
</Text>
<Parse>
(ROOT
	(S
	  (NP  (NNP Arnor) (JJ cleric))
	  (VP (VBZ is)
		(VP (IN about)
		  (S
			(VP (TO to)
			  (VP (VB restore)
				(NP (JJ full) (JJ diplomatic) (NNS ties))
				(PP (IN with)
				  (NP (NNP Gondor)))
				(SBAR
				  (NP (RB almost) (CD five) (NNS years))
				  (IN after)
				  (S
					(NP (NNS crowds))
					(VP (VBD trashed)
					  (NP (PRP$ its) (NN embassy)))))))))))
    (. .)))
</Parse>
</Sentence>
